      <script>
       function setCookie(cookieName, valCookie, valDomain) {
        var setDateCookies = '365';       //12 mesi alla scadenza da oggi, parametro espresso in giorni
        var expire = new Date();
        expire.setDate(expire.getDate() + parseInt(setDateCookies));
        document.cookie = cookieName + '=' + escape(valCookie) + '; expires=' + expire.toGMTString() + '; path=/; Domain='+valDomain;
    }
    function readCookie(cookieName) {
        if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
            var start = document.cookie.indexOf(cookieName + "=");
            if (start != -1) {
                start = start + cookieName.length + 1;
                var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";",start);
                if (end == -1) end = document.cookie.length;
                return unescape(document.cookie.substring(start,end));
            } else {
                return "";
            }
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    }
    var domain = window.location.hostname;
    var popupSeen = "popupVisto";
    var adformcookie = "adformcookie";
    var omniturecookie = "omniturecookie";
    var domain_code = 1022;
    if (domain == "www.tim.it") { domain_code = 1022; }
    if (domain == "alpha.tim.it") { domain_code = 1026; }
    function cookieManager(seen, adform, omniture) {
        //nascondo la barra dei cookie
        $("#cookie-policy-bar").hide();
        //stacco i 3 cookie
        if(adform){
            setCookie(adformcookie, adform, domain);
        }
        setCookie(popupSeen, seen, domain);
        setCookie(omniturecookie, omniture, domain);
        //popolo l'oggetto digitalData con il riferimento al cookie
        if(window.OmnitureController){
            OmnitureController.setOmnitureCookie(omniture);
        }

        if(window.Adform && Adform.Opt){
            if(adform) {
                Adform.Opt.optIn(domain_code, function () {
                    console.log("AdForm: OptIn eseguito");
                });
                Adform.Opt.disableRedirect();
            }else {
                window.location.href = '/web-privacy-policy';
            }
        }else{
            if(!adform){
                window.location.href = '/web-privacy-policy';
            }
        }
        //se siamo in pagina in cui Ã¨ presente il toggle, aggiorno anche quello
        if($(".toggle-trigger-cookie").length > 0){
            $(".toggle-trigger-cookie").prop('checked', omniture);
        }
        //elimino l'event listener
        document.removeEventListener('click', clickHandler);
    }

    function clickHandler(e){
        console.log("clicked", e.target);
        var el = $(e.target);
        if(el.parents('#cookie-policy-bar').length <= 0 && (el.is('a') || el.is('button') || el.is('input'))){
            //se clicco fuori dalla barra
            cookieManager(true, true, true);
        }
    }
    var init = function () {
        if(!readCookie(popupSeen)){
            document.addEventListener('click', clickHandler);
            var cookieBarRoot = $('#cookie-policy-bar');
            cookieBarRoot.show();
            cookieBarRoot.on("click", ".to-cookie-bar__close", function () {
                cookieManager(true, true, true);
            });
            cookieBarRoot.on("click", ".to-cookie-bar__buttons .ta-button.-primary", function () {
                cookieManager(true, true, true);
            });
            cookieBarRoot.on("click", ".to-cookie-bar__buttons .ta-button.-tertiary", function () {
                cookieManager(true, true, true);
            });
            cookieBarRoot.on("click", ".to-cookie-bar__scopri", function () {
                cookieManager(true, undefined, false);
            });
        }
    }();
      </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var pm = parseInt("307530");
  </script>
  <script onload="window.onAdFormLoad ? onAdFormLoad() : ''" src="https://track.adform.net/serving/scripts/trackpoint/" type="text/javascript">
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   var sessionExpirationTime = 1440;
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   window.disableGetAdFormParameters = false;
        window.enableAdFormTrackForHash = '';
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   function trueHashFooter() {
            if(window.location.hash){
                if(window.location.hash.indexOf('#/') == 0 || window.location.hash.indexOf("=") > -1) {
                    return '';
                }else{
                    return window.location.hash;
                }
            }else{
                return '';
            }
        }

        function setOmnitureUser(sv5,tiid) {
            if(window.getAdFormParametersVersion == '/api/v2/getAdformParameters' && window.digitalData){
                if(!digitalData.user){
                    digitalData["user"]={}
                }

                if(sv5 && sv5 != ''){
                    digitalData.user["cli"] = sv5;
                }

                if(tiid && tiid != ''){
                    digitalData.user["tiid"] = tiid;
                }
            }
        }

        if (!window.disableGetAdFormParameters && window.disableGetAdFormParameters == false) {
            var orderForAdFormFooter = {};
            var dateNew = window.performance.now();

            var diffMs = Math.abs(dateNew - window.sessionStorage.getItem('dateForAdFormParameters'));
            var minutes = Math.floor(((diffMs % 86400000) %  3600000) / 60000);
            var diffMinutesTime = minutes ? minutes : 0;

            if (!window.sessionStorage.getItem('dateForAdFormParameters') || diffMinutesTime >= sessionExpirationTime) {
                getOrderIp2CliFooter(dateNew);
            } else {
                getAdFormSessionStorageItemFooter();
            }

        } else {
            if(window.getAdFormLocation){
                trackPage(pm, getAdFormLocation(window.enableAdFormTrackForHash) );
            }else{
                console.warn("getAdFormLocation not found");
            }
        }

        function getAdFormLocation(hashParameter) {
            var adFormLocation = window.location.protocol + '//' + window.location.hostname + (window.location.port ? ":" + window.location.port : "") + window.location.pathname;
            if(hashParameter && hashParameter !== '' && window.location.hash.indexOf("#"+hashParameter) === 0){
                return adFormLocation = adFormLocation + window.location.hash;
            }
                return adFormLocation;
        }
        
        function trackPage(pm, location, order) {
            window._adftrack = Array.isArray(window._adftrack) ? window._adftrack : (window._adftrack ? [window._adftrack] : []);
            if (order) {
                window._adftrack.push({
                    pm: pm,
                    divider: encodeURIComponent('|'),
                    pagename: encodeURIComponent(location),
                    order: order
                });
            } else {
                window._adftrack.push({
                    pm: pm,
                    divider: encodeURIComponent('|'),
                    pagename: encodeURIComponent(location)
                });
            }
            (function () { var s = document.createElement('script'); s.type = 'text/javascript'; s.async = true; s.src = 'https://track.adform.net/serving/scripts/trackpoint/async/'; var x = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; x.parentNode.insertBefore(s, x); })();
            console.log("AdForm Tracciamento pagina: ", getAdFormLocation(window.enableAdFormTrackForHash) )
        }

        function getAdFormSessionStorageItemFooter () {
            var adFormParameters = window.sessionStorage.getItem('AdFormParameters');
            if(window.getAdFormLocation) {
                if (adFormParameters) {
                    adFormParameters = JSON.parse(adFormParameters);
                    setOmnitureUser(adFormParameters.sv5, adFormParameters.tiid);
                    trackPage(pm, getAdFormLocation(window.enableAdFormTrackForHash), adFormParameters);
                } else {
                    trackPage(pm, getAdFormLocation(window.enableAdFormTrackForHash));
                }
            }else{
                console.warn("getAdFormLocation not found");
            }
        }

        function getOrderIp2CliFooter (dateNew) {
            var responseObservable = Ip2CliService.getAdFormParameters();
            responseObservable.subscribe({
                next:function(response){
                    if(response){
                        window.sessionStorage.setItem('dateForAdFormParameters', dateNew);
                        orderForAdFormFooter = getMappedParameters(response.response);

                        setOmnitureUser(orderForAdFormFooter.sv5, orderForAdFormFooter.tiid);

                        window.sessionStorage.setItem('AdFormParameters', JSON.stringify(orderForAdFormFooter));
                        if(window.getAdFormLocation) {
                            trackPage(pm, getAdFormLocation(window.enableAdFormTrackForHash), orderForAdFormFooter);
                        }else{
                            console.warn("getAdFormLocation not found");
                        }
                    }
                },error: function(response) {
                    console.log('Error Ip2CliService');
                    if(window.getAdFormLocation){
                        trackPage(pm, getAdFormLocation(window.enableAdFormTrackForHash) );
                    }else{
                        console.warn("getAdFormLocation not found");
                    }
                }
            });
        }
  </script>
